Servicio Web De Gestion De Reservas

 Regression (tag)

 Happy Paths (tag)

Creacion, busqueda de una reserva usando la fecha de checkin
 

Cast

  Administrador del gestor de reservas

Administrador del gestor de reservas can:
  • call an API at https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com

Scenario Outline

Given que el usuario admin crea una reserva para un cliente llega el "<checkin>" y se va el "<checkout>" con un "<additionalneeds>"
Then el sistema debera de traer la reserva cuando la busca con filtro de checkin

Examples: 

# Checkin Checkout Additionalneeds
1 2013-02-02 2023-02-12 Lunch
2 1021-12-02 2023-11-12 Sea
3 0022-21-02 2023-02-10 Beer
Steps Outcome
1: Creacion, busqueda de una reserva usando la fecha de checkin ({checkin=2013-02-02, checkout=2023-02-12, additionalneeds=Lunch})
SUCCESS 1s 980ms
Given que el usuario administrador obtenien el token de seguridad
SUCCESS 495ms
Administrador del gestor de reservas auth token
SUCCESS 489ms
Administrador del gestor de reservas executes a POST on the resource /auth
SUCCESS 481ms
POST https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com/auth

Response

URL: https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com/auth

Status code: 200

Content Type: application/json

Request Headers

Accept=*/*
Content-Type=application/json; charset=UTF-8

Content Body

{
    "password": "password123",
    "username": "admin"
}

Response Headers

Server: Cowboy
Connection: keep-alive
X-Powered-By: Express
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
Content-Length: 27

Via: 1.1 vegur

Given que el usuario admin crea una reserva para un cliente llega el "2013-02-02" y se va el "2023-02-12" con un "Lunch"
SUCCESS 535ms
Administrador del gestor de reservas create booking
SUCCESS 530ms
Administrador del gestor de reservas executes a POST on the resource /booking
SUCCESS 511ms
POST https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com/booking

Response

URL: https://restful-booker.herokuapp.com/booking

Status code: 200

Content Type: application/json

Request Headers

Accept=*/*
Content-Type=application/json; charset=UTF-8

Content Body

{
    "firstname": "Archonei",
    "additionalneeds": "Lunch",
    "bookingdates": {
        "checkin": "2013-02-02",
        "checkout": "2023-02-12"
    },
    "totalprice": 4,
    "depositpaid": true,
    "lastname": "Royce of the Gates of the Moon"
}

Response Headers

Server: Cowboy
